cmake_minimum_required(VERSION 3.7)

set(CMAKE_SYSTEM_NAME Generic)
set(CMAKE_TRY_COMPILE_TARGET_TYPE STATIC_LIBRARY)
set(CMAKE_C_COMPILER arm-none-eabi-gcc)
set(CMAKE_CXX_COMPILER arm-none-eabi-g++)
set(CMAKE_ASM_COMPILER arm-none-eabi-gcc)

project(dwm1001_blinky VERSION 0.0.0 LANGUAGES C CXX ASM)

SET(CMAKE_C_FLAGS_BACKUP  "${CMAKE_C_FLAGS}")
SET(CMAKE_CXX_FLAGS_BACKUP  "${CMAKE_CXX_FLAGS}")
SET(CMAKE_ASM_FLAGS_BACKUP  "${CMAKE_ASM_FLAGS}")

set_property(SOURCE apps/blinky/src/main.c APPEND_STRING
														PROPERTY
														COMPILE_FLAGS
														"-DAPP_NAME=blinky -DAPP_blinky -DARCH_NAME=cortex_m4 -DARCH_cortex_m4 -DBSP_NAME=dwm1001 -DBSP_dwm1001 -DMYNEWT=1 -DNRF52 -Og -Wall -Werror -fdata-sections -ffunction-sections -fno-exceptions -ggdb -mcpu=cortex-m4 -mthumb -mthumb-interwork")
# Generating CMakeLists.txt for apps/blinky

add_library(apps_blinky apps/blinky/src/main.c)

							LIBRARY_OUTPUT_DIRECTORY bin/targets/dwm1001_blinky/app/apps/blinky
